       105 ( 0.00%)      pub fn stable_cmp(&self, tcx: TyCtxt<'tcx>, other: &Self) -> Ordering {

       108 ( 0.00%)          match (*self, *other) {
         .                       (Trait(_), Trait(_)) => Ordering::Equal,
